                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2012/10/genetically-modified-foods-depopulation.html">
                      Genetically Modified Foods, Depopulation, and Prop. 37
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content">
                     <i>
                      In earlier times it was easier to control a million people than  physically to kill a million people. Today it is infinitely easier to  kill a million people then to control a million people. -
                     </i>
                     <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HRMGI-STUdY">
                      Zbigniew Brzezinski
                     </a>
                     (CFR, Trilateral Commission, Bilderberg, Carter/Obama Advisor).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: right;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bHpFDuwVM6o/UHL9FHFkETI/AAAAAAAADLA/dKDeEYjnblw/s1600/GMO+Rats.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="116" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bHpFDuwVM6o/UHL9FHFkETI/AAAAAAAADLA/dKDeEYjnblw/s200/GMO+Rats.jpg" width="200"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     Paul Adams, J.D.
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2012/10/genetically-modified-foods-depopulation.html">
                      <b>
                       Activist Post
                      </b>
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Research and studies demonstrate that Genetically Modified (GM) foods potentially serve two purposes, neither of which is to feed the starving masses or
                     <a href="http://responsibletechnology.org/docs/gm-crops-do-not-increase-yields.pdf">
                      increase crop yield
                     </a>
                     on a long-term basis.  Instead, the purposes of GM foods appear to be those of a bad science-fiction nightmare:
                     <br/>
                     <ol>
                      <li>
                       Reduce the human population by
                       <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MSpkLk0vYmk">
                        poisoning the food supply
                       </a>
                       , causing increases in cancer, inflammation, disease, organ failure and premature death.  At the same time, using food to covertly render the population infertile.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Give a handful of elites and the companies they control complete control over the worlds food supply.
                      </li>
                     </ol>
                     As
                     <a href="http://www.globalresearch.ca/doomsday-seed-vault-in-the-arctic/">
                      Henry Kissinger said
                     </a>
                     , If you control the oil you control the country; if you control the food, you control the population.
                     <a href="http://www.historyplace.com/worldhistory/genocide/stalin.htm">
                      Joseph Stalin
                     </a>
                     agreed and is infamous for starving millions of people to death and submission.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     With their accomplices at the
                     <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=h0CQrL5nzwo">
                      Food and Drug Administration (FDA)
                     </a>
                     and within governments, a few
                     <a href="http://www.gmwatch.org/gm-firms/10558-the-worlds-top-ten-seed-companies-who-owns-nature">
                      corporate giants
                     </a>
                     and their major investors are responsible for much of the damage, destruction, and injuries caused by GM foods.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a name="more">
                     </a>
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monsanto_Corporation">
                      Monsanto
                     </a>
                     and Dow Chemical manufacture GM seeds and toxic herbicides such as
                     <a href="http://articles.mercola.com/sites/articles/archive/2012/01/15/dr-don-huber-interview-part-2.aspx">
                      Roundup (Glyphosate)
                     </a>
                     .  These two corporations also produced
                     <a href="http://naturalsociety.com/outrageous-agent-orange-maker-monsanto-seeks-return-to-vietnam-for-gmo-crops/">
                      Agent Orange
                     </a>
                     herbicide. Vietnam estimates 400,000 people were killed or maimed, and 500,000 children born with birth defects as a result of Agent Orange. The Red Cross of Viet Nam estimates that up to 1 million people are disabled or have health problems due to Agent Orange.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div align="center">
                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       google_ad_client = "pub-1897954795849722";
/* 468x60, created 6/30/10 */
google_ad_slot = "8230781418";
google_ad_width = 468;
google_ad_height = 60;
                      </script>
                      <script src="http://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js" type="text/javascript">
                      </script>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     Dow Chemical was also the manufacturer of
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napalm#Effects_on_people">
                      Napalm
                     </a>
                     , which was used to burn the skin off children like
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phan_Thi_Kim_Phuc">
                      Phan Thi Kim Phuc
                     </a>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Why are these corporate criminals being allowed to take over the worlds food supply?  Money and corruption would be the obvious answers, but after reviewing the evidence objectively and without cognitive dissonance, depopulation and control over the worlds food supply prove more likely.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                      Studies Prove GM Foods and Roundup Lethal
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The recent and
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2012/09/gmo-global-alert-truth-has-been-revealed.html">
                      long-term French study
                     </a>
                     from the University of Caen found that eating genetically modified corn and consuming trace levels of Monsanto's Roundup chemical fertilizer caused rats to develop horrifying tumors, widespread organ damage, and premature death. This study has been deemed "the most thorough research ever published into the health effects of GM food crops and the herbicide Roundup on rats."
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://www.biolsci.org/v05p0706.htm">
                      The study found
                     </a>
                     :
                     <br/>
                     <ul>
                      <li>
                       Up to 50% of males and 70% of females suffered
                       <b>
                        premature death.
                       </b>
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Rats that drank trace amounts of Roundup (at levels legally allowed in the water supply) had a
                       <b>
                        200% to 300% increase in large tumors.
                       </b>
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Rats fed GM corn and traces of Roundup suffered
                       <b>
                        severe organ damage
                       </b>
                       including liver damage and kidney damage.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       The study fed these rats
                       <b>
                        NK603
                       </b>
                       , the Monsanto variety of GM corn that's grown across North America and widely fed to animals and humans. This is the same corn that's in your
                       <a href="http://www.naturalnews.com/037315_Monsanto_GM_corn_breakfast_cereals.html">
                        corn-based breakfast cereal
                       </a>
                       , corn tortillas and corn snack chips.
                      </li>
                     </ul>
                     The study caused
                     <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2208452/Russia-suspends-import-use-American-GM-corn-study-revealed-cancer-risk.html">
                      Russia to ban imports of U.S. GM corn
                     </a>
                     due to the cancer risk.  France and most of Europe have effectively banned feeding GM crops to humans and Monsanto was found
                     <a href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2012/02/13/france-pesticides-monsanto-idINDEE81C0FQ20120213">
                      guilty of chemical poisoning
                     </a>
                     earlier this year.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://activistpost.net/stepoutsidethebox.html" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                      <img alt="" src="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-kADbI3spO2M/TwILKt_It9I/AAAAAAAANvU/F0N-dw_gGR4/s261/cancer.png"/>
                     </a>
                     In the Unites States,
                     <a href="http://www.cancer.org/Cancer/CancerBasics/lifetime-probability-of-developing-or-dying-from-cancer">
                      one in two men and one in three women
                     </a>
                     get cancer.  What role does GM corn and soy play, which are common in most processed foods?
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://www.naturalnews.com/035029_GM_corn_Walmart_Monsanto.html">
                      Walmart sells GM corn
                     </a>
                     to its customers without labeling it as such.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Russian biologist Alexey V. Surov, and his colleagues were determined to discover if
                     <a href="http://www.responsibletechnology.org/article-gmo-soy-linked-to-sterility">
                      Monsanto's genetically modified soy
                     </a>
                     , grown on 91% of US soybean fields, leads to problems in growth or reproduction.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     They found that after feeding hamsters for two years over three generations, those on the GM diet, and especially the group on the maximum GM soy diet, showed devastating results. By the third generation, most GM soy-fed hamsters lost the ability to have babies. They also suffered slower growth, and a high mortality rate among the pups.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Scientific studies have linked Monsantos
                     <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2010/01/12/monsantos-gmo-corn-linked_n_420365.html">
                      GM corn to organ failure
                     </a>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Other studies have linked
                     <a href="http://www.agoracosmopolitan.com/news/health/2011/10/23/1304.html">
                      GM foods to cancer
                     </a>
                     . Monsantos GM-derived rBGH (which is a genetically-altered growth hormone given to dairy cows to make them more milk) was shown to increase the production of IGF-1 from 70-1000%. IGF-1 is a very powerful hormone that has been linked to a 2.5-4 times higher incidence of human colon,
                     <a href="http://www.ethicalinvesting.com/monsanto/bgh.shtml">
                      breast and prostate cancer
                     </a>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Even
                     <a href="http://www.pakalertpress.com/2012/02/11/monsanto-employees-dont-even-eat-gmos/">
                      Monsantos employees refuse to eat GM foods
                     </a>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     As the Health Ranger opined, GM foods appear to be the
                     <a href="http://www.naturalnews.com/037178_thalidomide_apology_victims.html">
                      new Thalidomide
                     </a>
                     , that morning sickness drug from the late 1950s that was quickly recalled for its deadly side effects.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     It must also be noted that
                     <a href="http://www.sott.net/articles/show/237064-GMO-Researchers-Attacked-Evidence-Denied-and-a-Population-at-Risk">
                      world famous researchers
                     </a>
                     that expose the dangers of GM foods are routinely
                     <a href="http://www.scientistsunderattack.com/">
                      threatened, fired, ostracized
                     </a>
                     and their findings denied by
                     <a href="http://www.naturalnews.com/037440_Proposition_37_Henry_Miller_Stanford_University.html">
                      questionable experts with conflicts of interest
                     </a>
                     .  Studies proving GM food health risks are also
                     <a href="http://rt.com/news/corn-study-gm-french-711/">
                      routinely rejected
                     </a>
                     by bought-and-paid-for government officials.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     For many years
                     <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=P5B62cbwP_E">
                      Jeffrey Smith
                     </a>
                     has been exposing the dangers of GM foods combined with government corruption.  Much of his research can be viewed at the
                     <a href="http://www.responsibletechnology.org/resources/media-kit/jeffrey-m-smith-bio">
                      Institute for Responsible Technology
                     </a>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                      GMO Corruption and Conflicts of Interest
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Why are foods that contain GM ingredients allowed to be sold in the U.S. and Canada without a warning or disclaimer?  Corruption.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The global elite and their political puppets tell the public that toxic GM food is safe while they themselves are
                     <a href="http://www.motherjones.com/tom-philpott/2012/09/report-monsanto-man-mitt-romney-eats-organic">
                      obsessed with eating only organic foods
                     </a>
                     .  It is well known that the Clintons, Bush family, Romney family and Obamas try to eat only organic foods.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Dozens of
                     <a href="http://www.biointegrity.org/list.html">
                      FDA scientists warned
                     </a>
                     that GM crops were dangerous and different from traditional crops only to be disregarded by their superiors such as Michael Taylor at the FDA.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2012/03/monsanto-fdas-michael-taylor-to-keynote.html">
                      Michael Taylor
                     </a>
                     was an attorney at King &amp; Spalding that started working for Monsanto in 1981. In 1991 he filled the newly created post of Deputy Commissioner for Policy at the FDA. During that time, he signed the Federal Register notice stating that milk from cows treated with
                     <a href="http://www.preventcancer.com/consumers/general/milk.htm">
                      Bovine Growth Hormone (BGH) did not have to be labeled
                     </a>
                     as such. Between 1996 and 2000, after briefly returning to King &amp; Spalding, he then returned to Monsanto to become Vice President for Public Policy. In June of 2000 he joined the think tank Resources for the Future in the position of Senior Fellow and Director of RFFs Center for Risk Management, where he published two documents on U.S. aid for African agriculture, both of which were funded by the
                     <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kaiser_Wilhelm_Institute_of_Anthropology,_Human_Heredity,_and_Eugenics">
                      Rockefeller Foundation
                     </a>
                     , known for financing Nazi eugenics.  In 2009 Taylor returned to government as Senior Advisor to the FDA Commissioner and on in 2010 was appointed to FDA Deputy Commissioner for Foods.  In other words,
                     <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/jeffrey-smith/youre-appointing-who-plea_b_243810.html">
                      the fox is guarding the chickens
                     </a>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://activistpost.net/superfoods.html" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                      <img alt="" src="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-3r6MC2eTURY/UF4PWCetL1I/AAAAAAAARz0/qsSSnRnWLNQ/s220/200-2.jpg"/>
                     </a>
                     Dozens of high ranking government officials, including Secretary of State Hillary Clinton,
                     <a href="http://www.organicconsumers.org/monsanto/">
                      have ties with Monsanto
                     </a>
                     .  However, it could be argued that Barack Obama may be
                     <a href="http://jonrappoport.wordpress.com/2012/09/24/meet-monsantos-number-one-lobbyist-barack-obama/">
                      Monsantos number one lobbyist
                     </a>
                     because he filled many key USDA and FDA posts with Monsanto minions.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But dont expect the other side of the false left vs. right divide and conquer paradigm to save you;
                     <a href="http://thinkprogress.org/election/2012/09/14/850321/romney-monsanto/?mobile=nc">
                      Mitt Romney is also a Monsanto stooge
                     </a>
                     :
                     <br/>
                     <blockquote class="tr_bq">
                      The Nations
                      <a href="http://www.thenation.com/article/169885/mitt-romney-monsanto-man">
                       investigative report
                      </a>
                      has uncovered how Mitt Romney personally helped Monsanto shed its string of toxic chemical-related scandals and reinvent itself to dominate American agriculture. Monsanto, an early Bain &amp; Company client, was so impressed with Romney that they started bypassing his superiors to deal with him directly. Romneys close relationship with then CEO John Hanley prompted his boss to create Bain Capital to keep Romney from leaving and taking their largest consulting client with him.
                     </blockquote>
                     Whole Foods has been
                     <a href="http://www.wholefoodsmarket.com/blog/lets-talk-about-gmos-whole-foods-market">
                      caught in a scandal
                     </a>
                     because its employees are trained to tell customers the grocery chain sells only organic foods.  In fact, Whole Foods also sells toxic GM foods.
                     <br/>
                     <blockquote class="tr_bq">
                      Whole Foods co-founder and
                      <a href="http://www.opensecrets.org/usearch/index.php?q=john+mackey&amp;searchButt_clean.x=0&amp;searchButt_clean.y=0&amp;cx=010677907462955562473%3Anlldkv0jvam&amp;cof=FORID%3A11">
                       CEO John Mackey donated
                      </a>
                      to Mitt Romney, who helped
                      <a href="http://www.infowars.com/romneys-first-project-with-bain-in-1977-help-propel-monsanto/">
                       promote Monsantos entry into biotechnology
                      </a>
                      , while
                      <a href="http://fundrace.huffingtonpost.com/neighbors.php?type=name&amp;oldest=1&amp;lname=Robb&amp;fname=Walter&amp;search=Search+Names">
                       co-CEO Walter Robb donated
                      </a>
                      to Barack Obama, who has
                      <a href="http://www.infowars.com/meet-monsantos-number-one-lobbyist-barrack-obama/">
                       appointed numerous Monsanto lobbyists
                      </a>
                      to his administration, as well as
                      <a href="http://www.infowars.com/obamas-agriculture-secretary-supports-gmo-crops-big-agra/">
                       Christie Vilsack, the wife of USDA chief Tom Vilsack
                      </a>
                      , who as an Iowan politician, has bent over backward for biotech, GMOs, cloning and even the open-air growing of pharmaceutical crops.
                     </blockquote>
                     The GM food issue has once again revealed that the mainstream media is a corporate whore easily purchased by the ugliest and most degenerate Johns.  In
                     <a href="http://www.sacbee.com/2012/10/02/4874832/no-on-prop-37-in-case-you-missed.html">
                      recent editorials
                     </a>
                     , nine more California newspapers joined the growing list of publications urging voters to oppose Proposition 37 [requiring that GM foods be labeled as such) on the November ballot.  At least 29 mindless and corrupt newspapers endorse voting no on Proposition 37.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Unfortunately, Matt Drudge, the undisputed king of online news with his Drudge Report, has accepted advertising from the vote no on Proposition 37 campaign and features such ads regularly.  Therefore Drudge, just like the
                     <a href="http://www.freepress.net/ownership/chart">
                      corporate whore media
                     </a>
                     oligarchy, has revealed himself as a
                     <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judas_Iscariot">
                      modern day Judas Iscariot
                     </a>
                     who sold-out his family, country and humanity to a group of psychopathic eugenicists hell-bent on poisoning the food supply in their Malthusian quest to reduce the population.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                      The Depopulation Agenda
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     It is no longer a secret that the global elites
                     <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=x-CrNlilZho">
                      endgame
                     </a>
                     is to
                     <a href="http://endoftheamericandream.com/archives/from-7-billion-people-to-500-million-people-the-sick-population-control-agenda-of-the-global-elite">
                      reduce the human population by 80-95 percent
                     </a>
                     .  They even build monuments like the
                     <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_NA7-o1gGXI">
                      Georgia Guidestones
                     </a>
                     stating such.  What better way could there be than to
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2010/07/7-secret-ways-we-are-being-poisoned.html">
                      poison the food supply
                     </a>
                     without people knowing it?  Profit and depopulation.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Prominent university Professors such as
                     <a href="http://www.prisonplanet.com/articles/april2006/030406massculling.htm">
                      Eric Pianka
                     </a>
                     and
                     <a href="http://www.infowars.com/uc-professor-eyes-permanent-sterilant-to-cull-us-population/">
                      Richard Cardullo
                     </a>
                     openly crave depopulation.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://activistpost.net/ultimatesurvivalplan.html" style="float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;" target="_blank">
                      <img alt="" src="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-CTsdDqKcvhI/T7GjToaksaI/AAAAAAAAO2s/8vEb9HmqOhk/s316/160x316.gif"/>
                     </a>
                     Obamas top science and technology advisor
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2012/04/haters-of-humanity-church-of-malthus.html">
                      John P. Holdren
                     </a>
                     , advocated the formation of a planetary regime that would use a global police force to
                     <a href="http://www.activistpost.com/2012/03/un-policy-paper-outlines-7-building.html">
                      enforce totalitarian measures
                     </a>
                     of population control, including forced abortions, mass sterilization programs conducted via the food and water supply, as well as mandatory bodily implants that would prevent couples from having children.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>

                     <b>
                      California Proposition 37  Require GM Food Labeling
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     California Proposition 37 is the wooden stake that California voters can drive through the GM food industrys criminal corporate hearts on November 6th.  If passed, it will require that products containing GM foods be labeled, which is akin to placing a skull and cross bones on the product. Because very few people are willing to knowingly eat GM foods, products containing them will likely be forced by consumer demand to replace GM ingredients to healthier and natural alternatives.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Proposition 37 is a ballot initiative, meaning that over 1,000,0000 people signed a petition to have labeling GM foods placed on the election ballot.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://www.mercola.com/">
                      Dr. Mercola
                     </a>

                     <a href="http://us.naturespath.com/">

                     <a href="http://articles.mercola.com/sites/articles/archive/2012/09/13/california-gmo-labeling.aspx">

                     </a>
                     financially.  They believe that GM foods should be labeled as they are in most of Europe, Russia, China, Japan, Australia, Brazil, India and many other countries.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     There are
                     <a href="http://www.naturalnews.com/037247_Proposition_37_California_label_GMOs.html">
                      dozens of reasons to support Proposition 37
                     </a>
                     and Californians can get more information at
                     <a href="http://www.carighttoknow.org/">
                      http://www.carighttoknow.org/
                     </a>
                     .  If approved by voters, the labeling initiative would make California the first state in the nation to require labels on genetically engineered crops or processed foods, such as corn, soybeans, sugar beets and Hawaiian papayas. Other states would likely follow.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Proposition 37 opponents have raised more than $32.5 million while Yes on 37 campaign had raised $3.5 million. Despite the financial disparity,
                     <a href="http://www.latimes.com/business/la-fi-prop37-times-poll-20120927,0,5015236.story">

function mce_success_cb(resp){
    mce_jQuery('#mce-success-response').hide();
    mce_jQuery('#mce-error-response').hide();
    if (resp.result=="success"){
        mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
        mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(resp.msg);
        mce_jQuery('#mc-embedded-subscribe-form').each(function(){
            this.reset();
     });
    } else {
        var index = -1;
        var msg;
        try {
            var parts = resp.msg.split(' - ',2);
            if (parts[1]==undefined){
                msg = resp.msg;
            } else {
                i = parseInt(parts[0]);
                if (i.toString() == parts[0]){
                    index = parts[0];
                    msg = parts[1];
                } else {
                    index = -1;
                    msg = resp.msg;
                }
            }
        } catch(e){
            index = -1;
            msg = resp.msg;
        }
        try{
            if (index== -1){
                mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
                mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(msg);            
            } else {
                err_id = 'mce_tmp_error_msg';
                html = '&lt;div id="'+err_id+'" style="'+err_style+'"&gt;

 '+msg+'&lt;/div&gt;
';
                var input_id = '#mc_embed_signup';
                var f = mce_jQuery(input_id);
                if (ftypes[index]=='address'){
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index]+'-addr1';
                    f = mce_jQuery(input_id).parent().parent().get(0);
                } else if (ftypes[index]=='date'){
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index]+'-month';
                    f = mce_jQuery(input_id).parent().parent().get(0);
                } else {
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index];
                    f = mce_jQuery().parent(input_id).get(0);
                }
                if (f){
                    mce_jQuery(f).append(html);
                    mce_jQuery(input_id).focus();
                } else {
                    mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
                    mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(msg);
                }
            }
        } catch(e){
            mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
            mce_jQuery('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(msg);
        }
    }
}

                       <p>
                        GM food doesn't cause cancer. Herbicides and pesticides cause cancer. Your crazy conspiracy theories are just that.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        Everyone knows that herbicides and pesticides cause cancer. This is not a surprise to anyone. Get a large enough dose ("trace amounts" is a deliberate lie - the actual dose is relative to body weight, and while it seems small, that's true of most toxins) and you will get cancer or die. Its just the nature of the beast.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        But GM foods are not the cause of this. The cause is modern agricultural practices that allow us to produce food more efficiently
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        Whine all you want, but GM foods are not dangerous - people like you, however, are. You are dangerously misinformed and you don't understand the science behind this stuff.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        The key is not "eliminate GM foods" but "develop foods that require the least amount of the least toxic chemical possible to get good results". Washing fruit and vegetables before you eat them or before you prepare them is important; likewise, companies are expected to do the same.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        Your alarmism is pointless. The reason we have the FDA is to ensure that toxic doses of chemicals do not enter the food stream. Your paranoia about GM foods is misplaced.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        Measure 37 is a scaremongering tactic brought up by crazy people like yourself.
                       </p>
                      </dd>

                      <dt class="comment-author " id="c3717586875211794194">
                       <a name="c3717586875211794194">
                       </a>
                       <div class="avatar-image-container avatar-stock">
                        <span dir="ltr">
                         <img alt="" height="16" src="http://img1.blogblog.com/img/blank.gif" title="Anonymous" width="16"/>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       Anonymous
said...
                      </dt>
                      <dd class="comment-body" id="Blog1_cmt-3717586875211794194">
                       <p>
                        "GM food doesn't cause cancer."
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        The French study demonstrated much higher rates of cancer in rats that ate GM corn untreated with glyphosate.  This is the only long term GM feeding study to date.  Where is your long term feeding study data to contradict this?
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        Several short term studies analyzing the effects of a GM diet on the cellular level found inflammation, altered cell signaling, and mutations in developing animal fetuses.  These cellular level changes are consistent with initiator and promoter aspects of carcinogens - thus setting up the conditions for the development of dysplasia/cancer.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        "You are dangerously misinformed and you don't understand the science behind this stuff."
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        Tell that to the esteemed Arpad Pusztai.  I am also a medical scientist.  Regardless, a scientific background in not necessary to add 2 and 2 together.  Provide average people with accurate information and a basic education on GMOs and the majority will get it.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        BTW, Unknown, the disinfo tactics and buzzwords are getting pretty old: "crazy conspiracy theories", "alarmism", "scaremongering", "paranoia"
                       </p>
                      </dd>

                  function recentpostslist(json) {
 document.write('&lt;ul&gt;');
 for (var i = 0; i &lt; json.feed.entry.length; i++)
 {
    for (var j = 0; j &lt; json.feed.entry[i].link.length; j++) {

        break;

    }
